	; RECEIVE
	; RE1:
	; MOV TEMP_HEAD_X , 200
	; MOV TEMP_HEAD_Y , 300
	; MOV TEMPHEAD , OFFSET FIRE
	; CALL DRAW_HEAD
	; CMP value , 'A'
	; JNZ RE1
	; ; 18 SNAKE1_X
	; MOV CX , 18
	; MOV BX , 0
	; LR1:
	; PUSH BX
	; PUSH CX
	; RECEIVE
	; MOV AL , VALUE
	; MOV BYTE PTR SNAKE1_X[BX] , AL
	; POP CX
	; POP BX
	; INC BX
	; LOOP LR1

	RE1:                        
	                            RECEIVE
	                            CMP     value , 'A'
	                            JNZ     RE1
	; 18 SNAKE1_X
	                            MOV     CX , 18
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR1:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE1_X[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR1

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'B'
	; JNZ RE1
	; 18 SNAKE1_Y
	                            MOV     CX , 18
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR2:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE1_Y[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR2

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'C'
	; JNZ RE1

	; 18 SNAKE2_X
	                            MOV     CX , 18
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR3:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE2_X[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR3

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'D'
	; JNZ RE1
	; 18 SNAKE2_Y
	                            MOV     CX , 18
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR4:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE2_Y[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR4

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'E'
	; JNZ RE1

	; 4 LEN_ARR
	                            MOV     CX , 4
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR5:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE_LEN_ARR[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR5

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'F'
	; JNZ RE1
	; 2 SCORE1
	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR6:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR PLAYER1_SCORE[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR6

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'G'
	; JNZ RE1

	; 2 SCORE2
	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR7:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR PLAYER2_SCORE[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR7

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'H'
	; JNZ RE1

	; SECONDS
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     VALUE, AL
	                            MOV     DISPLAYED_SECONDS , AL

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'I'
	; JZ RE1
	;MINS
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     DISPLAYED_MINUTES  ,AL

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'J'
	; JNZ RE1

	; 2 INDEX_FIRE
	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR8:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR CURR_FIRE_INDEX[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR8

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'K'
	; JNZ RE1
	; 2 INDEX_APPLE
	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR9:                        
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR CURR_APPLE_INDEX[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR9

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'L'
	; JNZ RE1
	; 2 SNAKE1_HEAD_DIR
	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR10:                       
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE1_HEAD_DIRECTION[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR10

	; RECEIVE
	; CMP value , 'M'
	; JNZ RE1


	; 2 SNAKE2_HEAD_DIR
	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR11:                       
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE2_HEAD_DIRECTION[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR11

	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR12:                       
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR END_OF_THE_GAME[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR12

	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR13:                       
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE1_FREEZE[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR13

	                            MOV     CX , 2
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	LR14:                       
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     AL , VALUE
	                            MOV     BYTE PTR SNAKE2_FREEZE[BX] , AL
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            INC     BX
	                            LOOP    LR14

	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     VALUE, AL
	                            MOV     NUM_TO_GET_GOLDEN , AL

	                            RECEIVE
	                            MOV     VALUE, AL
	                            MOV     open_chat , AL

	                            RET
	

RECEIVE_DATA ENDP




PRINT_TIME2 PROC NEAR
	PRINT_CURR_TIME2:           
	                            MOV     AL,DISPLAYED_MINUTES
	                            MOV     MINUTES,AL
	                            MOV     AL,DISPLAYED_SECONDS
	                            MOV     SECONDS,AL
	;mov  al, seconds              	;;;divide if seconds two digit
	                            mov     bh,10
	                            mov     ah,00
	                            div     bh
	                            mov     temp_sec2,ah
	                            mov     temp_sec1,al

	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;print minute;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                            mov     dl,22h
	                            mov     dh,1h                                                 	;row
	                            mov     bh,0
	                            mov     ah,02h
	                            int     10h
	                            mov     bl,1                                                  	;color
	                            mov     al,minutes
	                            add     al,30h
	                            mov     ah,0eh                                                	;
	                            int     10h

	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;print colon;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;print colon;;;;;


	                            mov     dl,23h                                                	;column
	                            mov     ah,02h
	                            int     10h
	                            mov     al,3ah
	                            mov     ah,0eh                                                	;
	                            int     10h
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;print second;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                            mov     dl,24h                                                	;column
	                            mov     ah,02h
	                            int     10h
	                            mov     al, temp_sec1
	                            add     al,30h
	                            mov     ah,0eh                                                	;
	                            int     10h
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;second digit;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                            mov     dl,25h                                                	;column
	                            mov     ah,02h
	                            int     10h
	                            mov     al,temp_sec2
	                            add     al,30h
	                            mov     ah,0eh                                                	;
			
	                            int     10h


	                            JMP     END_PRINT_TIME_PROC2

	TIME_OUT2:                  
	                    

	END_PRINT_TIME_PROC2:       

	                            RET
PRINT_TIME2 ENDP


DELETE_FOR_PLAYER2 PROC NEAR
	                            MOV     SI,OFFSET APPLE_X
	                            MOV     BX, TEMP_CURR_APPLE_INDEX
	                            MOV     DX, [SI+BX]
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_X ,DX

	                            MOV     SI,OFFSET APPLE_Y
	                            MOV     BX, TEMP_CURR_APPLE_INDEX
	                            MOV     DX, [SI+BX]
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_Y ,DX
			 
	                            MOV     TEMP_COLOR, BGC
	                            CALL    DRAW_SQUARE
	                            MOV     SI,OFFSET FIRE_X
	                            MOV     BX, TEMP_CURR_FIRE_INDEX
	                            MOV     DX, [SI+BX]
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_X ,DX

	                            MOV     SI,OFFSET FIRE_Y
	                            MOV     BX, TEMP_CURR_FIRE_INDEX
	                            MOV     DX, [SI+BX]
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_Y ,DX
			 
	                            MOV     TEMP_COLOR, BGC
	                            CALL    DRAW_SQUARE
								
	                            MOV     CX , TEMP_SNAKE1_X[0]
	                            MOV     DX , TEMP_SNAKE1_Y[0]
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_X ,CX                                     	;set the initial column (X)
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_Y ,DX                                     	;set the initial line (Y)
	                            MOV     TEMP_COLOR , BGC
	                            CALL    DRAW_SQUARE
	                            MOV     CX , TEMP_SNAKE_LEN_ARR[0]
	                            SUB     CX , 1
	                            MOV     BX , 2
	                            MOV     TEMP_COLOR, BGC
	DELETE_BODY_SQUARES:        
							   
	                            MOV     AX, TEMP_SNAKE1_X[BX]
	                            MOV     DX , TEMP_SNAKE1_Y[BX]
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_X ,AX                                     	;set the initial column (X)
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_Y ,DX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            CALL    DRAW_SQUARE
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            ADD     BX , 2
	                            LOOP    DELETE_BODY_SQUARES

	                            MOV     CX , TEMP_SNAKE2_X[0]
	                            MOV     DX , TEMP_SNAKE2_Y[0]
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_X ,CX                                     	;set the initial column (X)
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_Y ,DX                                     	;set the initial line (Y)
	                            MOV     TEMP_COLOR , BGC
	                            CALL    DRAW_SQUARE
	                            MOV     CX , TEMP_SNAKE_LEN_ARR[2]
	                            SUB     CX , 1
	                            MOV     BX , 2
	                            MOV     TEMP_COLOR, BGC
	DELETE_BODY2_SQUARES:       
							   
	                            MOV     AX, TEMP_SNAKE2_X[BX]
	                            MOV     DX , TEMP_SNAKE2_Y[BX]
	                            PUSH    BX
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_X ,AX                                     	;set the initial column (X)
	                            MOV     INIT_SQUARE_Y ,DX
	                            PUSH    CX
	                            CALL    DRAW_SQUARE
	                            POP     CX
	                            POP     BX
	                            ADD     BX , 2
	                            LOOP    DELETE_BODY2_SQUARES
	                            RET
DELETE_FOR_PLAYER2 ENDP

	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
MOVE_SNAKE PROC NEAR

	START:                      
	BEG:                        
	;Check that Data is Ready
	                            mov     dx , 3FDH                                             	; Line Status Register
	                            in      al , dx
	                            test    al , 1
	                            JZ      CHK                                                   	;Not Ready (This line may need to change)
	;If Ready read the VALUE in Receive data register
	                            mov     dx , 03F8H
	                            in      al , dx
	                            mov     VALUE , al
	                            MOV     AH , VALUE
	                            JMP     BEG1
	CHK:                        
	                            mov     ah,1
	                            int     16h
	                            JNZ     BEG2
	                            JMP     BEG
	BEG2:                       
	                            mov     ah,0
	                            int     16h
	BEG1:                       
						
	                            CMP     AH ,72
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                            CMP     AH ,80
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                            CMP     AH,77
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                            CMP     AH,75
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                   
							
	         
	                            CMP     AH ,11H
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                            CMP     AH ,1FH
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                            CMP     AH,20H
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP
	                            CMP     AH,1EH
	                            JZ      SNAKE_1_HELP

	                            JMP     START


	SNAKE_1_HELP:               
	                            JMP     SNAKE_1

	NEW_START:                  

	; CALL SEND_DATA
	; mov bl , 1
	; add to_send , bl

	                            CALL    Print_time
	                            CALL    DRAW_APPLE
	                            CALL    CHECK_FOOD
	                            CALL    DRAW_FIRE
	                            CALL    CHECK_FIRE
	                            CALL    print_score_player1
	                            CALL    print_score_player2
	                            CALL    CHECK_BITE
	                            CALL    ONE_IS_FREEZED
	                            CALL    TWO_IS_FREEZED
	                            CALL    DRAW_SNAKES
	                            CALL    SEND_DATA
	                            CMP     END_OF_THE_GAME,0
	                            JNZ     RETURN_TO_MAIN_HELP_HELP
								

	                            CMP     NUM_C_EAT_SNAKE1 , 3
	                            JE      FREEZE_SNAKE2
	                            CMP     NUM_C_EAT_SNAKE2,3
	                            JNE     END_OF_FREEZE_CHECKING
	                            MOV     NUM_C_EAT_SNAKE2,0
	                            MOV     DX, POWER_UP1_PENALITY
	                            MOV     SNAKE1_FREEZE,DX
	                            JMP     END_OF_FREEZE_CHECKING
								
	FREEZE_SNAKE2:              
	                            MOV     NUM_C_EAT_SNAKE1,0
	                            MOV     DX, POWER_UP1_PENALITY
	                            MOV     SNAKE2_FREEZE,DX
	END_OF_FREEZE_CHECKING:     

	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;DELAY MACRO ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                            MOV     CX,0000H
	                            MOV     DX,LVL_SPEED
	                            MOV     AH,86H
	                            INT     15H
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;


	;Check that Data is Ready
	                            mov     dx , 3FDH                                             	; Line Status Register
	                            in      al , dx
	                            test    al , 1
	                            JZ      CHK1                                                  	;Not Ready (This line may need to change)
	;If Ready read the VALUE in Receive data register
	                            mov     dx , 03F8H
	                            in      al , dx
	                            mov     VALUE , al
	                            MOV     AH , VALUE
	                            JMP     AS_GETTING_KEY
	CHK1:                       
	                            MOV     AH,1
	                            INT     16h
	                            JZ      GO_AS_BEFORE

	                            MOV     AH,0
	                            INT     16H
								
	                            CMP     AH ,11H
	                            JZ      player1_pressed_wsad
	                            CMP     AH ,1FH
	                            JZ      player1_pressed_wsad
	                            CMP     AH,20H
	                            JZ      player1_pressed_wsad
	                            CMP     AH,1EH
	                            JZ      player1_pressed_wsad
	                            jmp     skip_player1_pressed_wsad

	player1_pressed_wsad:       
	                            mov     ah,TEMP_BUFFER1
	skip_player1_pressed_wsad:  
	AS_GETTING_KEY:             
                               
	SNAKE_1:                    
	
	                            CMP     AH ,3EH
	                            JZ      RETT
	                            CMP     AH,3CH
	                            JZ      game_chat
	                            JMP     CONTIN
	RETT:                       
	                            mov     END_OF_THE_GAME,1
	                            CALL    SEND_DATA
	                            RET
	game_chat:                  
	                            cmp     value , 3ch
	                            jz      ignore_send
	                            mov     open_chat , 1
	                            call    send_data
	ignore_send:                
	                            call    inline_chat
	                            mov     open_chat , 0
	                            call    send_data
	CONTIN:                     
	                            CMP     AH ,72
	                            JZ      UP1_HELP_HELP
	                            CMP     AH ,80
	                            JZ      DOWN1_HELP_HELP
	                            CMP     AH,77
	                            JZ      RIGHT1_HELP_HELP
	                            CMP     AH,75
	                            JZ      LEFT1_HELP_HELP

	                       


	SNAKE_2:                    
	                            CMP     AH ,11H
	                            JZ      UPDATE_TEMP_BUFFER2
	                            CMP     AH ,1FH
	                            JZ      UPDATE_TEMP_BUFFER2
	                            CMP     AH,20H
	                            JZ      UPDATE_TEMP_BUFFER2
	                            CMP     AH,1EH
	                            JZ      UPDATE_TEMP_BUFFER2


	                            JMP     GO_AS_BEFORE



	RETURN_TO_MAIN_HELP_HELP:   
	                            JMP     RETURN_TO_MAIN_HELP
	UP1_HELP_HELP:              
	                            JMP     UP1_HELP

	RIGHT1_HELP_HELP:           
	                            JMP     RIGHT1_HELP

	DOWN1_HELP_HELP:            
	                            JMP     DOWN1_HELP
	

	LEFT1_HELP_HELP:            
	                            JMP     LEFT1_HELP

	




	UPDATE_TEMP_BUFFER2:        
	                            MOV     TEMP_BUFFER2,AH
	                            MOV     AH,TEMP_BUFFER1
	                            JMP     SNAKE_1


	GO_AS_BEFORE:               

								
	;CMP  SNAKE1_FREEZE,0
	;JNE  SNAKE1_IS_FREEZED

	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER1 ,72
	                            JZ      UP1
	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER1 ,80
	                            JZ      DOWN1
	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER1,77
	                            JZ      RIGHT1
	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER1,75
	                            JZ      LEFT1

	                   
	SNAKE2_LABEL:               

	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER2 ,11H
	                            JZ      UP2_HELP_HELP
	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER2 ,1FH
	                            JZ      DOWN2_HELP_HELP
	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER2,20H
	                            JZ      RIGHT2_HELP_HELP
	                            CMP     TEMP_BUFFER2,1EH
	                            JZ      LEFT2_HELP_HELP

	;SNAKE2_IS_FREEZED:
	;  DEC  SNAKE2_FREEZE
	                            JMP     NEW_START                                             	;

	UP1_HELP:                   
	                            JMP     UP1
	DOWN1_HELP:                 
	                            JMP     DOWN1
	LEFT1_HELP:                 
	                            JMP     LEFT1
	RIGHT1_HELP:                
	                            JMP     RIGHT1
	UP2_HELP_HELP:              
	                            JMP     UP2_HELP

	DOWN2_HELP_HELP:            
	                            JMP     DOWN2_HELP

	RIGHT2_HELP_HELP:           
	                            JMP     RIGHT2_HELP

	LEFT2_HELP_HELP:            
	                            JMP     LEFT2_HELP

	RETURN_TO_MAIN_HELP:        
	                            JMP     RETURN_TO_MAIN


	UP1:                        
	      
	                            CMP     SNAKE1_FREEZE , 0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_UP1
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE1_UP
	                            MOV     TEMP_BUFFER1,72
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL
	SKIP_UP1:                   
	                            DEC     SNAKE1_FREEZE
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL

	DOWN1:                      
	                            CMP     SNAKE1_FREEZE , 0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_DOWN1
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE1_DOWN
	                            MOV     TEMP_BUFFER1,80
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL
	SKIP_DOWN1:                 
	                            DEC     SNAKE1_FREEZE
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL

	RIGHT1:                     
	                            CMP     SNAKE1_FREEZE , 0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_RIGHT1
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE1_RIGHT
	                            MOV     TEMP_BUFFER1,77
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL
	SKIP_RIGHT1:                
	                            DEC     SNAKE1_FREEZE
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL
	LEFT1:                      
	                            CMP     SNAKE1_FREEZE , 0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_LEFT1
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE1_LEFT
	                            MOV     TEMP_BUFFER1,75
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL
	SKIP_LEFT1:                 
	                            DEC     SNAKE1_FREEZE
	                            JMP     SNAKE2_LABEL

	                    
	UP2_HELP:                   
	                            JMP     UP2
	DOWN2_HELP:                 
	                            JMP     DOWN2
	LEFT2_HELP:                 
	                            JMP     LEFT2
	RIGHT2_HELP:                
	                            JMP     RIGHT2





	UP2:                        
	                            CMP     SNAKE2_FREEZE,0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_UP2
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE2_UP
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	SKIP_UP2:                   
	                            DEC     SNAKE2_FREEZE
	                            JMP     NEW_START
	DOWN2:                      
	                            CMP     SNAKE2_FREEZE,0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_DOWN2
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE2_DOWN
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	SKIP_DOWN2:                 
	                            DEC     SNAKE2_FREEZE
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	RIGHT2:                     
	                            CMP     SNAKE2_FREEZE,0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_RIGHT2
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE2_RIGHT
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	SKIP_RIGHT2:                
	                            DEC     SNAKE2_FREEZE
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	LEFT2:                      
	                            CMP     SNAKE2_FREEZE,0
	                            JNZ     SKIP_LEFT2
	                            CALL    MOVE_SNAKE2_LEFT
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	SKIP_LEFT2:                 
	                            DEC     SNAKE2_FREEZE
	                            JMP     NEW_START

	RETURN_TO_MAIN:             
	                            RET
MOVE_SNAKE ENDP

MOVE_SNAKE_P2 PROC NEAR

	START_MOVE2:                

	                            MOV     AH,1
	                            INT     16h
	                            JZ      LLL
	                            MOV     AH,0
	                            INT     16h
	                            MOV     value,ah
								
	                            CMP     value ,72
	                            JZ      LLL
	                            CMP     value ,80
	                            JZ      LLL
	                            CMP     value,77
	                            JZ      LLL
	                            CMP     value,75
	                            JZ      LLL
	;Check that Transmitter Holding Register is Empty
	                            mov     dx , 3FDH                                             	; Line Status Register
	AGAIN1:                     In      al , dx                                               	;Read Line Status
	                            test    al , 00100000b
	                            JZ      AGAIN1                                                	;Not empty (This line may need to change)
	;If empty put the VALUE in Transmit data register
	                            mov     dx , 3F8H                                             	; Transmit data register
	                            mov     al,VALUE
	                            out     dx , al
	                            cmp     value , 3ch
	                            jz      inline_chat_call
	                            jmp     LLL
	inline_chat_call:           call    inline_chat
	LLL:                        
	; CMP  END_OF_THE_GAME,0
	; JNZ  RETURN_FROM_THE_FUNC
	;call delete_snakes
	;call delete_for_player2
	                            MOV     AX , CURR_APPLE_INDEX
	                            MOV     TEMP_CURR_APPLE_INDEX , AX
	                            MOV     AX , CURR_FIRE_INDEX
	                            MOV     TEMP_CURR_FIRE_INDEX , AX
	                            MOV     AX , SNAKE_LEN_ARR[0]
	                            MOV     TEMP_SNAKE_LEN_ARR[0],AX
	                            MOV     AX , SNAKE_LEN_ARR[2]
	                            MOV     TEMP_SNAKE_LEN_ARR[2],AX

	                            MOV     CX , 10
	                            MOV     BX , 0
	TEMP_SNAKE1:                
	                            MOV     AX , SNAKE1_X[BX]
	                            MOV     TEMP_SNAKE1_X[BX] , AX
	                            MOV     AX , SNAKE1_Y[BX]
	                            MOV     TEMP_SNAKE1_Y[BX] , AX
	                            MOV     AX , SNAKE2_X[BX]
	                            MOV     TEMP_SNAKE2_X[BX] , AX
	                            MOV     AX , SNAKE2_Y[BX]
	                            MOV     TEMP_SNAKE2_Y[BX] , AX
	                            ADD     BX , 2
	                            LOOP    TEMP_SNAKE1

	                            call    RECEIVE_DATA
	                            cmp     open_chat,1
	                            jz      inline_chat_call2
	                            jmp     ccc
	inline_chat_call2:          call    inline_chat
	ccc:                        
	                            CMP     END_OF_THE_GAME,0
	                            JNZ     RETURN_FROM_THE_FUNC
	;CALL    DRAW_BACK_G
	                            call    DELETE_FOR_PLAYER2
	; mov     bx , init_square_y
	; mov     dx , init_square_x
	; mov    player1_score , bx

	; mov     ah , temp_color
	; call    DRAW_SQUARE

	                            CALL    PRINT_TIME2
	                            CALL    DRAW_APPLE
	                            CALL    DRAW_FIRE
	                            CALL    ONE_IS_FREEZED
	                            CALL    TWO_IS_FREEZED
	                            CALL    print_score_player1
	                            CALL    print_score_player2

	                            CALL    DRAW_SNAKES
	                            MOV     CX,0000H
	                            MOV     DX,00FFH
	                            MOV     AH,86H
	                            INT     15H


	                            JMP     START_MOVE2
	; 18 SNAKE1_X
	; 18 SNAKE1_Y
	; 18 SNAKE2_X
	; 18 SNAKE2_Y
	; 4 LEN_ARR
	; 2 SCORE1
	; 2 SCORE2
	; 2 SECONDS
	; 2 MINS
	; 2 INDEX_FIRE
	; 2 INDEX_APPLE
	; 2 SNAKE1_HEAD_DIR
	; 2 SNAKE2_HEAD_DIR
	; DRAW SNAKE 1
	; DRAW SNAKE 2
	; DRAW APPLE
	; DRAW FIRE
	; DRAW TIME
	; DRAW SCORE



	RETURN_FROM_THE_FUNC:       
	                            RET
MOVE_SNAKE_P2 ENDP
inline_chat proc near                                                                      		;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;to do inline chat
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;clear the area to write;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	begin_again:                 
	                             mov     cx,900
	                             mov     dx,1500h
	clear_area:                  mov     bh,0
	                             mov     ah,02h
	                             int     10h
    
	;score of player 1
	                             mov     bl,0                                                  	;color
	                             mov     al,0
	;  add  al,2eh
	                             mov     ah,0eh                                                	;
			
	                             int     10h
	                             inc     dx
	                             loop    clear_area
	;HORIZONTAL
	                             mov     ah,0CH
	                             MOV     CX,640
	LP:                          
	                             CMP     CX,320
	                             JL      CHANGE_COLOR
	                             MOV     AL,02H
	                             JMP     COLOR_CHANGED
	CHANGE_COLOR:                
	                             MOV     AL,05H
	COLOR_CHANGED:               
	                             MOV     BH,0
	                             MOV     DX,335                                                	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                             INT     10H
	                             LOOP    LP

	;HORIZONTAL
	                             mov     ah,0CH
	                             MOV     CX,640
	LP2:                         
	                             CMP     CX,320
	                             JL      CHANGE_COLOR2
	                             MOV     AL,02H
	                             JMP     COLOR_CHANGED2
	CHANGE_COLOR2:               
	                             MOV     AL,05H
	COLOR_CHANGED2:              
	                             MOV     BH,0
	                             MOV     DX,350                                                	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                             INT     10H
	                             LOOP    LP2

	;VERTICAL
	                             MOV     AH,0CH
	                             MOV     DX,335
	LP3:                         
	                             MOV     CX,320
	                             MOV     BH,0
	                             MOV     AL,07H
	                             INT     10H
	                             INC     DX
	                             CMP     DX,400
	                             JNZ     LP3


	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	;print_name1



	                             mov     si,offset name_s2+4
	
	                             mov     dx,1500h
	                             mov     bl , 5
	                             call    player_p
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;print_name2
	                             mov     si,offset name_s+4
	                             mov     dx,152ch
	                             mov     bl , 2
	                             call    player_p

	
	
	;  mov  ah,0
	; int  16h
	                             mov     counter_chat,0
	                             mov     counter_chat2,0

	                             mov     inc_dh,0
	                             mov     inc_dh2,0

	inf2:                        


	            

	                             cmp     counter_chat2,35


	                             jnz     check_next_area
	                             cmp     inc_dh2,2
	                             jnz     cont_inc
	                             jmp     begin_again

	
	cont_inc:                    inc     inc_dh2
	                             mov     counter_chat2,0



	check_next_area:             cmp     counter_chat,35
	                             jnz     con

	                             cmp     inc_dh,2
	                             jnz     inc_positions
	                             jmp     begin_again
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                           


    
	;score of player 1

	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;




	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	inc_positions:               inc     inc_dh
	                             mov     counter_chat,0

	con:                                                                                       	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;scrolling

	; mov     ah, 7
	; mov     al, 0
	; mov     cx, 1600h
	; mov     dh, 4fh
	; mov     dl, 18h
	; mov     bh, 12h
	; int     10h

	; ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	; cmp player_num ,1
	; jz P_is_1
	                             mov     ah,2
	                             mov     bh , 0
								
	                             cmp     player_num ,1

	                             jz      P_is_1
	                             mov     dx,1600h
	                             add     dh,inc_dh
	                             add     dl,counter_chat
	                             jmp     end_of_setup
	P_is_1:                      
	                             mov     dx,162ch
	                             add     dh,inc_dh2
	                             add     dl,counter_chat2
	end_of_setup:                
	
	                             int     10h

	;jmp s_p_is_1
	;;;;;;;;;;if press key
	; P_is_1:
	; mov     ah,2
	;                             mov     bh , 0
	;                             mov     dx,162ch
	; 							add     dh,inc_dh
	;                             add     dx,counter_chat
								  
	                           
	; s_p_is_1:
	                             mov     ah,1
	                             int     16h
	                             jz      re2
	                             mov     ah,0
	                             int     16h
	; cmp al,1bh ;ESC key
	  
	; jz exit2
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;printing
	                             mov     ah,2
	                             mov     dl,al
	                             mov     VALUE,al

	                             cmp     value,1bh
	                             jz      exit3
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;backspace;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;


	;int 21h
	;;;;;;;;;;;;

	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                        

	not_backspace_in_inlinechat: 


	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                             mov     ah,09
	                             mov     bh,0
	                             mov     al,value
	                             mov     cx,1h
	                             mov     bl,3
	                             int     10h
	                             cmp     player_num ,1
	                             jz      P_is_1_inc_counter
	                             inc     counter_chat
	                             jmp     skip1
	p_is_1_inc_counter:          
	                             inc     counter_chat2
	skip1:                       
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                             mov     dx , 3FDH                                             	; Line Status Register
	AGAIN2:                      In      al , dx                                               	;Read Line Status
	                             test    al , 00100000b
	                             JZ      AGAIN2

	;If empty put the VALUE in Transmit data register
	                             mov     dx , 3F8H                                             	; Transmit data register
	                             mov     al,VALUE
	                             out     dx , al
	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;transmit
	;;;;;;;set cursor


	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	re2:                         

	;Check that Data is Ready
	                             mov     dx , 3FDH                                             	; Line Status Register
	                             in      al , dx
	                             test    al , 1
	                             JZ      CK2                                                   	;Not Ready
	;If Ready read the VALUE in Receive data register
	                             mov     dx , 03F8H
	                             in      al , dx
	                             mov     VALUE , al
	                             cmp     value , 1bh
	                             jz      exit3
	                             cmp     player_num ,1
	                             jz      is_p_1_2
	                    
	                             cmp     counter_chat2,35
	                             jnz     con2
	                             Jz      inc_col2
	inc_col2:                    
	                             inc     inc_dh2
	                             mov     counter_chat2,0
	                             jmp     skip2
	is_p_1_2:                    

	                             cmp     counter_chat,35
	                             jnz     con2
	                             Jz      inc_col2_2
	inc_col2_2:                  
	                             inc     inc_dh
	                             mov     counter_chat,0

	skip2:                       


	
	con2:                        
	                             cmp     player_num ,1
	                             jz      P_is_1_r
	                             mov     ah,2
	                             mov     bh , 0
	                             mov     dx,162ch
	                             add     dl,counter_chat2
								  
	                             add     dh,inc_dh2
								
	                             int     10h
	                             jmp     s_p_is_1_r
	; ;;;;;;;;;;if press key
	; P_is_1_2:
	; mov     ah,2
	;                             mov     bh , 0
	;                             mov     dx,1600h
	;                              add     dx,counter_chat2
								  
	;                             add     dh,inc_dh2
	p_is_1_r:                    
	                             mov     ah,2
	                             mov     bh , 0
	                             mov     dx,1600h
	                             add     dl,counter_chat
								  
	                             add     dh,inc_dh
								
	                             int     10h

	s_p_is_1_r:                  

	                             mov     ah,2
	                             mov     al , value
	                             mov     dl,al
									
								
	                             mov     VALUE,al

	;int 21h
	                             mov     ah,09
	                             mov     bh,0
	                             mov     al,value
	                             mov     cx,1h
	                             mov     bl,3

	                             int     10h
	                             cmp     player_num , 1
	                             jz      p_num_1
	                             inc     counter_chat2
	                             jmp     s_p_num_1
	p_num_1:                     
	                             inc     counter_chat
	s_p_num_1:                   
	CK2:                         
	                             jmp     inf2


	;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
	                             mov     ah,0
	                             int     16h


	exit3:                       
	                             mov     open_chat,0
	                             call    DRAW_BACK_G
	                             call    DRAW_APPLE
	                             call    DRAW_FIRE
	                             call    DRAW_SNAKES
	                             mov     ax,0
	                             mov     counter_chat,al
	                             mov     counter_chat2,AL
	                             mov     inc_dh,al
	                             mov     inc_dh2,al
	                             mov     value , 1bh
	                             send
	                             ret
inline_chat endp

END MAIN

Pac-Man

Código em Linguagem Assembly do jogo Pac-Man

                TITLE PACMAN
                .MODEL SMALL 
                .STACK 100H
                
                PRINTAR	MACRO	MATRIZ, COR, POSICAO_X, POSICAO_Y, LARGURA, TAMANHO
                
                    PUSH CX
                
                    MOV EIXO_X, 0
                    MOV EIXO_Y, 0
                    MOV DIMENSAO, 0
                    MOV LARGURA_TOTAL, 0
                    XOR SI,SI
                
                    MOV AL, COR
                    MOV EIXO_X, POSICAO_X
                    MOV EIXO_Y, POSICAO_Y
                    MOV DIMENSAO, TAMANHO
                    MOV LARGURA_TOTAL, LARGURA
                    LEA SI, MATRIZ
                
                    CALL PIXEL
                    
                    POP CX
                    
                    ENDM
                    
                .DATA
                ;========================================================================================================================================================================
                ;MENSAGENS
                
                    
                    
                    TITULO 			DB 	' PACMAN x8086 '
                    TITULO_LEN	EQU $-TITULO
                    TITULO_CENTER EQU 20 - (TITULO_LEN/2)
                    
                    DECISAO			DB	' Pressione espaco: '
                    DECISAO_LEN	EQU	$-DECISAO
                    DECISAO_CENTER EQU 20 - (DECISAO_LEN/2)
                    
                    SCORE			DB	' PONTOS: '

                    SCORE_CENTER EQU 20 - (SCORE_LEN/2)

                    pontos_LEN EQU $-pontos

                ;=====================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================
                .CODE                                                                                                                                                             
                MAIN PROC
                
                    MOV AX,@DATA
                    MOV DS,AX
                    MOV ES,AX	
                            
                    MOV AUX,48	;0
                    MOV AUX1,48	;0
                    MOV pontos,48;0
                    
                                
                    MOV AX, 13h   ;setando o modo de video  320X200
                    INT 10h
                    
                    CALL BEMVINDO	; mensagens de boas vindas 
                    
                    MOV AX, 1300h
                    MOV BX, 4
                    MOV BL,44H
                    MOV DH, 20;linha
                    MOV DL, DECISAO_CENTER ; coluna
                    MOV CX, DECISAO_LEN
                    LEA BP, DECISAO
                    INT 10h
                    
                    MOV AH, 1                   
                    INT 21H                      
                    
                    CALL CLS
                    
                    CALL USUARIO
                    
                    CALL CLS
                
                    CALL ESCOLHAMAPA
                    CALL CLS
                    
                SAI:
                    MOV AH ,4Ch
                    INT 21H
                MAIN ENDP
                ;===========================================================
                ;MOVIMENTACAO PACMAN
                MOVIMENTO_PACMAN PROC
                
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                    
                    CMP AL,'p'
                    JNE VAI
                    
                    DEC VIDAS
                    CALL PERDE_VIDA
                    RET
                    
                VAI:
                    CMP AL,'a'
                    JE ESQUERDA1
                        
                    CMP AL,'d'
                    JE DIREITA1
                        
                    CMP AL,'s'
                    JE BAIXO1
                    
                    CMP AL,'w'
                    JE CIMA1
                    
                    CMP AL,0dh
                    JE FIM
                    
                    RET
                        
                ESQUERDA1:
                    JMP ESQUERDA
                    
                DIREITA1:
                    JMP DIREITA
                    
                CIMA1:
                    JMP CIMA
                    
                BAIXO1:
                    JMP BAIXO
                    
                FIM:
                    CALL FECHAR		
                    
                FIME:
                    RET
                    
                ESQUERDA:
                    CMP BX,31
                    JE FIME
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    SUB BX,16
                    CALL COLISOES		;PAREDE
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    CMP AX,1
                    JE FIME
                    
                
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                    SUB	BX,8
                    ADD DX,8		
                    
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP DX
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    
                    CMP AX,2	;COMIDA
                    JE PONTO1
                    
                    CMP AX,3	;PASTILHA
                    JE PASTILHA1
                    
                    CMP AX,4	;GHOST
                    JNE N_MORRE1
                    
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JNB COMEUGHOST1
                    
                    DEC VIDAS
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,VIDAS
                    CMP CX,0
                    JB FIME
                    POP CX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL PERDE_VIDA
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                    
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                    JMP NAO_PONTO1
                
                COMEUGHOST1:
                    POP CX
                    INC AUX
                    JMP PONTO1
                PASTILHA1:
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    MOV CX,10
                    MOV FOGE,CX
                    POP CX
                PONTO1:
                    INC AUX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL ATUALIZA_SCORE
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                N_MORRE1:	
                NAO_PONTO1:
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240		;APAGA
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                    SUB BX,16
                    MOV MOV_X,BX
                    MOV MOV_Y,DX
                
                    PRINTAR PACMANFECHADO,44H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    CALL DELAY
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240	;APAGA
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANABERTOESQ,44H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    RET
                    
                FIMD:
                    
                    RET
                    
                DIREITA:
                    CMP BX,127
                    JE FIMD
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    ADD BX,16
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    CMP AX,1
                    JE FIMD
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                    ADD	BX,24
                    ADD DX,8
                    
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP DX
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    CMP AX,2	;COMIDA
                    JE PONTO2
                    
                    CMP AX,3	;PASTILHA
                    JE PASTILHA2
                    
                    CMP AX,4	;GHOST
                    JNE N_MORRE2
                    
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JNB COMEUGHOST2
                    
                    DEC VIDAS
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,VIDAS
                    CMP CX,0
                    JB FIMD
                    POP CX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL PERDE_VIDA
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                    
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                    JMP NAO_PONTO2
                    
                COMEUGHOST2:
                    POP CX
                    INC AUX
                    JMP PONTO2
                PASTILHA2:
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    MOV CX,10
                    MOV FOGE,CX
                    POP CX
                PONTO2:
                    INC AUX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    
                    CALL ATUALIZA_SCORE
                    
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                N_MORRE2:
                NAO_PONTO2:
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240		;APAGA
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                    ADD BX,16
                    MOV MOV_X,BX
                    MOV MOV_Y,DX
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANFECHADO,44H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    CALL DELAY
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240	;APAGA
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANABERTODIR,44H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    RET
                    
                FIMC:
                    RET
                    
                CIMA:
                    CMP DX,31
                    JE FIMC
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    SUB DX,16
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP DX
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    CMP AX,1
                    JE FIMC
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    MOV CX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                    ADD	BX,8
                    SUB DX,8
                    
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP DX
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    CMP AX,2	;COMIDA
                    JE PONTO3
                    
                    CMP AX,3	;PASTILHA
                    JE PASTILHA3
                    
                    CMP AX,4
                    JNE N_MORRE3
                    
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JNB COMEUGHOST3
                    
                    DEC VIDAS
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,VIDAS
                    CMP CX,0
                    JB FIMC
                    POP CX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL PERDE_VIDA
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                    
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                    JMP NAO_PONTO3
                
                COMEUGHOST3:
                        POP CX
                        INC AUX
                        JMP PONTO3
                PASTILHA3:
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    MOV CX,10
                    MOV FOGE,CX
                    POP CX
                PONTO3:
                    INC AUX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL ATUALIZA_SCORE
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                N_MORRE3:	
                NAO_PONTO3:
                    
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240	;APAGA
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX, MOV_Y
                    
                    SUB DX,16
                    MOV MOV_X,BX
                    MOV MOV_Y,DX
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANFECHADO,44H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    CALL DELAY
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240	;APAGA
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANABERTOCIMA,44H,BX,DX,15,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    RET
                FIMB:
                    RET
                    
                BAIXO:
                    CMP DX,159
                    JE FIMB
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    ADD DX,16
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP DX
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    CMP AX,1
                    JE FIMB
                    
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    MOV CX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                
                    ADD	BX,8
                    ADD DX,24
                    
                    CALL COLISOES
                    POP DX
                    POP BX
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    
                    CMP AX,2	;COMIDA
                    JE PONTO4	
                    
                    CMP AX,3
                    JE PASTILHA4
                    
                    CMP AX,4
                    JNE N_MORRE4
                    
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    CMP CX,0
                    JNB COMEUGHOST4
                    
                    DEC VIDAS
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,VIDAS
                    CMP CX,0
                    JB FIMB
                    POP CX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL PERDE_VIDA
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                    
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                    JMP NAO_PONTO4
                    
                COMEUGHOST4:
                        POP CX
                        INC AUX 
                        JMP PONTO4
                PASTILHA4:
                    PUSH CX
                    MOV CX,FOGE
                    MOV CX,10
                    MOV FOGE,CX
                    POP CX
                PONTO4:
                    INC AUX
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH DX
                    PUSH CX
                    CALL ATUALIZA_SCORE
                    POP AX
                    POP	BX
                    POP	CX
                    POP	DX
                
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    
                N_MORRE4:	
                NAO_PONTO4:
                    
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240	
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    MOV DX, MOV_Y
                    
                    ADD DX,16
                    MOV MOV_X,BX
                    MOV MOV_Y,DX
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANFECHADO,44H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    CALL DELAY
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    PRINTAR PACMANABERTOBAIXO,44H,BX,DX,15,240
                    MOV DX,MOV_Y
                    MOV BX,MOV_X
                    
                    RET
                MOVIMENTO_PACMAN ENDP
                ;==========================================================================================================================
                RAND PROC
                RANDGEN:         ; generate a rand no using the system time
                RANDSTART:
                    MOV AH, 00h  ; interrupts to get system time        
                    INT 1AH      ; CX:DX now hold number of clock ticks since midnight      
                
                    MOV AX, DX
                    XOR DX, DX
                    MOV CX, 5
                    DIV CX       ; here dx contains the remainder of the division - from 0 to 5
                   
                    RET
                RAND ENDP
                ;==========================================================================================================================
                MOVIMENTO_FANTASMA1 PROC
                    
                    CALL RAND 
                    MOV PRONDEVOU,DX
                    
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH CX
                    PUSH DX
                    
                    ADD BX,16 ; DIREITA
                    
                    CALL COLISOES	; VEJO O QUE TEM 
                    POP AX
                    POP BX
                    POP CX
                    POP DX
                
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    CMP BX,127
                    JE DESVIA1_1
                    CMP PRONDEVOU,1
                    JNE DESVIA1_1
                    JMP DIR
                    
                DESVIA1_1:
                    JMP DESVIA1
                    
                DIR:
                    CMP AX,1 
                    JE DESVIA1_1
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240 ; APAGA	
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    ADD BX,16
                
                    MOV GHOST_X,BX
                    MOV GHOST_Y,DX
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JA MEDOA
                    PRINTAR FANTASMACACADOR,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    RET
                    MEDOA:
                    PRINTAR FANTASMAASSUSTADO,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    DEC FOGE
                    RET
                DESVIA1:
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH CX
                    PUSH DX
                    
                    SUB DX,16 ; CIMA
                    
                    CALL COLISOES	; VEJO O QUE TEM 
                    POP AX
                    POP BX
                    POP CX
                    POP DX
                
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    CMP DX,31
                    JE DESVIA2_1
                    CMP PRONDEVOU,2
                    JNE DESVIA2_1
                    JMP CI
                    
                DESVIA2_1:
                    JMP DESVIA2
                    
                CI:
                    CMP AX,1 
                    JE DESVIA2_1
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240 ; APAGA
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    SUB DX,16
                    
                    MOV GHOST_X,BX
                    MOV GHOST_Y,DX
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JA MEDOB
                    PRINTAR FANTASMACACADOR,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    RET
                    MEDOB:
                    PRINTAR FANTASMAASSUSTADO,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    DEC FOGE
                    RET
                DESVIA2:
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH CX
                    PUSH DX
                    
                    ADD DX,16 ; BAIXO
                    
                    CALL COLISOES	; VEJO O QUE TEM 
                    POP AX
                    POP BX
                    POP CX
                    POP DX
                
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    CMP DX,159
                    JE DESVIA3_1
                    CMP PRONDEVOU,3
                    JNE DESVIA3_1
                    JMP BAI
                    
                DESVIA3_1:
                    JMP DESVIA3
                    
                BAI:
                    CMP AX,1 
                    JE DESVIA3_1
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    PRINTAR APAGA,00H,BX,DX,16,240 ; APAGA
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    ADD DX,16
                    
                    MOV GHOST_X,BX
                    MOV GHOST_Y,DX
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JA MEDOC
                    PRINTAR FANTASMACACADOR,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    RET
                    MEDOC:
                    PRINTAR FANTASMAASSUSTADO,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    DEC FOGE
                    RET
                    
                DESVIA3:
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    PUSH AX
                    PUSH BX
                    PUSH CX
                    PUSH DX
                    
                    SUB BX,16 ; ESQUERDA
                    
                    CALL COLISOES	; VEJO O QUE TEM 
                    POP AX
                    POP BX
                    POP CX
                    POP DX
                
                    MOV AX,BOOLEANA
                    ;CALL SAIDECIMAL
                    CMP BX,31
                    JE DESVIA4_1
                    CMP PRONDEVOU,4
                    JNE DESVIA4_1
                    JMP ESQ
                    
                DESVIA4_1:
                    JMP DESVIA4
                    
                ESQ:
                    CMP AX,1 
                    JE DESVIA4_1
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    PRINTAR APAGA,0D,BX,DX,16,240 ; APAGA
                    MOV BX,GHOST_X
                    MOV DX,GHOST_Y
                    SUB BX,16
                    
                    MOV GHOST_X,BX
                    MOV GHOST_Y,DX
                    CMP FOGE,0
                    JA	MEDOD
                    PRINTAR FANTASMACACADOR,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    RET
                    MEDOD:
                    PRINTAR FANTASMAASSUSTADO,4D,BX,DX,16,240
                    DEC FOGE
                    RET
                    
                DESVIA4:
                    
                    RET
                MOVIMENTO_FANTASMA1 ENDP
